    lemma onorm_oCauchy:
      fixes f::‹nat ⇒ ('a::real_normed_vector ⇒ 'b::real_normed_vector)› and l::‹'a⇒'b›
      assumes ‹⋀ n. bounded_linear (f n)› and ‹f ─onorm→ l› and ‹bounded_linear l›
      shows ‹oCauchy f›

    reduction of instantiation real_bounded :: (real_normed_vector, banach) "banach" to completeness_real_bounded
    
    completeness_real_bounded is in the file SEQ_bounded_operators.thy
    
    lemma completeness_real_bounded:
      fixes f :: ‹nat ⇒ ('a::real_normed_vector ⇒ 'b::banach)›
      assumes ‹∀n. bounded_linear (f n)› and ‹∀e>0. ∃M. ∀m≥M. ∀n≥M. onorm (λx. f m x - f n x) < e›
      shows ‹∃ l. bounded_linear l ∧ (λn. onorm (λx. f n x - l x)) ⇢ 0›

    isolation of the essential part in the proof of the completeness of real bounded operators
    
    lemma completeness_real_bounded:
      fixes f :: ‹nat ⇒ ('a::real_normed_vector ⇒ 'b::banach)›
      assumes ‹∀n. bounded_linear (f n)› and ‹∀e>0. ∃M. ∀m≥M. ∀n≥M. onorm (λx. f m x - f n x) < e›
      shows ‹∃L. bounded_linear L ∧
            (∀S. (∀x∈S. bounded_linear x) ⟶ open S ⟶ L ∈ S ⟶ (∀⇩F x in sequentially. f x ∈ S))›

    introduction of the notion of strong convergence
    
    definition strong_convergence:: "(nat ⇒ ('a::real_normed_vector ⇒'b::real_normed_vector)) ⇒ ('a⇒'b) ⇒ bool"
      where ‹strong_convergence f l = ( ( λ n. onorm (l - f n) ) ⇢ 0 )›
    
    abbreviation
      strong_convergence_abbr :: "(nat ⇒ ('a::real_normed_vector ⇒'b::real_normed_vector)) ⇒ ('a⇒'b) ⇒ bool"  ("((_)/ ─strong→ (_))" [60, 60] 60)
      where "f ─strong→ l ≡ ( strong_convergence f l ) "

    I finished the proof of Banach_Steinhaus
    
    theorem Banach_Steinhaus:
      fixes f :: ‹'c ⇒ ('a::{banach,perfect_space} ⇒ 'b::real_normed_vector)›
      assumes ‹⋀ n. bounded_linear (f n)›
        and  ‹⋀ x. ∃ M. ∀ n.  norm ((f n) x) ≤ M›
      shows  ‹∃ M. ∀ n. onorm (f n) ≤ M›

    proof of Sokal's lemma
    
    lemma Sokal_Banach_Steinhaus:
      fixes f :: ‹'a::{real_normed_vector, perfect_space} ⇒ 'b::real_normed_vector›
        and r :: real and x :: 'a
      assumes ‹r > 0› and ‹bounded_linear f›
      shows ‹(onorm f) * r ≤ Sup {norm (f y) | y. dist y x < r}›

commit 28781bb250ccfad8eb4ec111ce39d70a23b0b715
Author: José Manuel Rodríguez Caballero <37361666+josephcmac@users.noreply.github.com>
Date:   Mon Jun 24 04:06:40 2019 +0300

    I proved Sup_Ineq
    
    lemma Sup_Ineq:
      fixes f g :: ‹'a ⇒ real›
      assumes ‹∀ x ∈ S. f x ≤ g x› and ‹bdd_above (f ` S)›
        and ‹bdd_above (g ` S)›
      shows ‹Sup (f ` S) ≤ Sup (g ` S)›

        and ‹∀ ε > 0. ∃ N::nat. ∀ m ≥ N. ∀ n ≥ N. ∀ S::'a set. finite S ⟶ (∑ x∈S. ( cmod ( ((a m) x) - ((a n) x) ) )^2)  ≤ ε›
